               DataItemTable=Table36;

                                  CLEAR(FooterTotal);
                                  i:=0;
                                  K:=0;


                                  "PageNo.":=CurrReport.PAGENO;
                                END;

               ReqFilterFields=Document Type,No. }

    { 1102159002;1;DataItem;                 ;
               DataItemTable=Table37;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Document Type,Document No.,Line No.)
                                 ORDER(Ascending);
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN

                               //Count1 :="Sales Line".COUNT;
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN

                                     Section1:=TRUE;

                                  //====================Sales Line Body 1 - OnPreSection

                                  IF ("Sales Line"."Currency Code" = '')  THEN
                                      "Sales Line"."Currency Code":='idr';


                                  //====================Sales Line Body 1 - OnPostSection

                                  ExceptionalAcc:= FALSE;

                                  IF (("Sales Line"."No."=MasterCustomerPostingSetup."Freight+Insurance Account") AND
                                         ("Sales Line"."VAT %"=0) AND ("Sales Line"."VAT Prod. Posting Group"<> '')) THEN
                                    BEGIN
                                    FooterTotal[2]+="Sales Line"."Line Amount";
                                    ExceptionalAcc:= TRUE;
                                  //  CurrReport.SHOWOUTPUT(FALSE);
                                    Section1:=FALSE;
                                  END;



                                  IF (("Sales Line"."No."=MasterCustomerPostingSetup."Stamp Duty Account") AND
                                    ("Sales Line"."VAT %"=0)) THEN
                                    BEGIN
                                    FooterTotal[4]+="Sales Line"."Line Amount";
                                    ExceptionalAcc:= TRUE;
                                  //  CurrReport.SHOWOUTPUT(FALSE);
                                    Section1:=FALSE;

                                    END;



                                  IF (("Sales Line"."No."=MasterCustomerPostingSetup."Other Charges Account")AND
                                    ("Sales Line"."VAT %"=0) AND ("Sales Line"."VAT Prod. Posting Group"= '')) THEN
                                    BEGIN
                                    FooterTotal[5]+="Sales Line"."Line Amount";
                                    ExceptionalAcc:= TRUE;
                                  //  CurrReport.SHOWOUTPUT(FALSE);
                                    Section1:=FALSE;
                                    END;




                                  //>>05122013/VK/CR#022
                                  mastersetup.GET;
                                  IF COMPANYNAME = mastersetup."Company Name YIMM" THEN BEGIN
                                  MasterSetup2.GET;
                                    IF (("Sales Line"."No." = MasterSetup2."YIMM Sales Discount") OR ("Sales Line"."No." = MasterSetup2."YIMM Instancy Discount") OR
                                      ("Sales Line"."No." = MasterSetup2."YIMM Campaign Discount") OR
                                      ("Sales Line"."No." = MasterSetup2."YIMM Selling In Discount") OR
                                      ("Sales Line"."No." = MasterSetup2."YIMM Selling Out Discount") OR
                                      ("Sales Line"."No." = MasterSetup2."YIMM Others")) THEN BEGIN
                                        SalesDiscount += "Sales Line"."Line Amount";
                                        ExceptionalAcc := TRUE;
                                    //    CurrReport.SHOWOUTPUT(FALSE);
                                    Section1:=FALSE;
                                  //  MESSAGE('yes 1..');

                                    END;
                                  END;
                                  //<<05122013/VK/CR#022

                                  IF "Sales Line"."VAT %" = 100 THEN BEGIN
                                    ExceptionalAcc:= TRUE;
                                  //  CurrReport.SHOWOUTPUT(FALSE);
                                    Section1:=FALSE;

                                  END;


                                  IF NOT ExceptionalAcc THEN
                                    BEGIN
                                    FooterTotal[1]+="Sales Line"."Line Amount";
                                    i+=1;
                                    END;


                                  IF VatPercent=0 THEN
                                  VatPercent:="Sales Line"."VAT %";
                                  FooterTotal[3]+="Sales Line"."Outstanding Amount"-"Sales Line"."Line Amount";



                                  //deepa
                                  //Message(format(FooterTotal[4])+'   '+format(section1));
                                END;

               DataItemLink=Document Type=FIELD(Document Type),
                            Document No.=FIELD(No.) }

    { 1102159036;2;Column;DocumentType_SalesLine;
               SourceExpr="Sales Line"."Document Type" }

    { 1102159051;2;Column;DocumentNo_SalesLine;

    { 1102159039;1;DataItem;                 ;
               DataItemTable=Table2000000026;
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN

                               //MESSAGE('before...'+FORMAT(Integer.COUNT)+'   '+FORMAT(i));
                               Integer.RESET;

                                    IF (i<16) THEN
                                    Integer.SETRANGE(Integer.Number,1,16-i)
                               ELSE  IF (i > 16 ) OR (i <= 35) THEN
                                       Integer.SETRANGE(Integer.Number,1,35-i)
                                 ELSE IF i > 35 THEN
                                       Integer.SETRANGE(Integer.Number,1,i-35)

                                    ELSE BEGIN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP;
                                    END;


                                //MESSAGE('after...'+FORMAT(Integer.COUNT));


                               //UPG13R2DEV.begin
                               CountBlankLines:=Integer.COUNT;
                               //UPG13R2DEV.end
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN

                                  //UPG13R2DEV.begin
                                      i:=i+1;
                                    // message(format(i)+'  '+'hi..');
                                   K:=K+1;
                                  SHowVar:=TRUE;

                                  IF(K>CountBlankLines) THEN
                                  SHowVar:=FALSE;
                                  //UPG13R2DEV.end
                                END;

               OnPostDataItem=BEGIN

                                 //SHowVar:=false;

                              END;
                               }

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function
